 India successfully test-fired its state-of-the-art Scramjet rocket engine by joining select clubs from some countries
 vayumandal kii oxigen kaa istemaal karte hue ingine kaa prakshepan kiya gaya, jisase prakshepan kii laagat kai guna kam ho sakati he or hawa se oxigen lene vaale ingine dizin karne ke isro ke prayaas main madad mil sakati he
 The Indian Space Research Organization said that the first pilot mission of the Scramjet engine was successfully conducted at 6 am from the Satish Dhawan Space Center in Sriharikota, Andhra Pradesh
 isro ne mishan ko saamaanya lekin vayumandal se oxigen lekar chalane vaale aadhunik injanon ko dizin or vikaas karne ke prayaas main mahatvapurn mile kaa pathar bataaya
 India is the fourth country to perform launch tests of scramjet engines after the US, Russia and the European Space Agency
 isro ne kaha ki 12 ghante kii nirbaadh ulti ginati ke baad scramjet ingine ko lekar aadhunik praudyogiki yaan (etivi) ne subah chah baje udaan bhari or 300 second kii udaan sriharikota se kareeb 320 kilometre dur bengal kii khadi main samaapt hui
 According to ISRO, five critical phases of this launch were completed as planned
 sriharikota se udaan ke dauraan antarikshayan par safaltaapurvak najar rakhi gai
 ISRO stated that its designed scramjet engines use hydrogen as fuel and take oxygen from the atmosphere air as an oxidizer
 saamaanya taur par rocket ke injanon main dahan ke liye eendhan or oxikaarak donon hote hai
 Scramjet engines will also be used to operate isro's reusable launch vehicle at hypersonic speed
 bangalooru main hi maujuud raashtrapati pranab mukherjee ne safal pareekshan ke liye isro ko badhai di
 He tweeted, 'heartiest congratulations to ISRO on successful testing of future Scramjet rocket engines

 donon ore se aarope pratyarope ke daur shuru hai
 Rajdeep Sardesai, Consulting Editor of India Today Group, spoke exclusively to Mamta Banerjee, who went out in the election campaign on Thursday
 kya mamata banerjee agali pradhanmantri hongi? iske jawaab main mamata ne kaha ki ve chaahati hai ki desh surakshit bane

 is sawaal par mamata ne kaha, 'unke bare main ham koi jawaab nahin denge
